	craftRecipe PrepareRation
	{
	Time = 25,
	timedAction = UnPackSmallBag,
	Tags = InHandCraft;Cooking;CanBeDoneInDark,
	category = Cooking,
	xpAward = Cooking:1,
	OnCreate = Recipe.OnCreate.OnCreateRation,

	inputs
	{
		item 1 [SupportCorps.RationMREMCW;SupportCorps.RationMRECIV;SupportCorps.RationMRECamping;SupportCorps.RationMRERelief;] mappers[RationType],
	}

	outputs
	{
		item 1 mapper:RationType,
		item 1 SupportCorps.InstantJuicePacket_Ground,
	}

	itemMapper RationType
	{
		SupportCorps.RationMREMCW_Open 		= SupportCorps.RationMREMCW,
		SupportCorps.RationMRECIV_Open		= SupportCorps.RationMRECIV,
		SupportCorps.RationMRECamping_Open	= SupportCorps.RationMRECamping,
		SupportCorps.RationMRERelief_Open	= SupportCorps.RationMRERelief,
	}
	}

	craftRecipe OpenLQAlcohol
	{
	Time = 25,
	timedAction = UnPackSmallBag,
	Tags = InHandCraft;Cooking;CanBeDoneInDark,
	category = Cooking,
	xpAward = Cooking:1,

	inputs
	{
		item 1 [SupportCorps.SealedBeerLQ;SupportCorps.SealedMeadLQ;SupportCorps.SealedBerrywineLQ;SupportCorps.SealedWhiskeyLQ;SupportCorps.SealedVodkaLQ;SupportCorps.SealedGinLQ;SupportCorps.SealedWineLQ;SupportCorps.SealedWhiteWineLQ;] mappers[LQAlcoholType],
        item 1 [Base.BottleOpener;Base.BottleOpener_Keychain;Base.Multitool;],
	}

	outputs
	{
		item 1 mapper:LQAlcoholType,
	}

	itemMapper LQAlcoholType
	{
		SupportCorps.OpenedBeerLQ 		= SupportCorps.SealedBeerLQ,
		SupportCorps.OpenedMeadLQ		= SupportCorps.SealedMeadLQ,
		SupportCorps.OpenedBerrywineLQ	= SupportCorps.SealedBerrywineLQ,
		SupportCorps.OpenedWhiskeyLQ	= SupportCorps.SealedWhiskeyLQ,
		SupportCorps.OpenedVodkaLQ		= SupportCorps.SealedVodkaLQ,
		SupportCorps.OpenedGinLQ	= SupportCorps.SealedGinLQ,
		SupportCorps.OpenedWineLQ	= SupportCorps.SealedWineLQ,
		SupportCorps.OpenedWhiteWineLQ	= SupportCorps.SealedWhiteWineLQ,
	}
	}	
					
	craftRecipe OpenAlcohol
	{
	Time = 25,

	}

craftRecipe MakeWoodenKeg
{
    Time = 25,
    timedAction = UnPackSmallBag,
    Tags = InHandCraft;Cooking;CanBeDoneInDark,
    category = Cooking,
    xpAward = Cooking:1,
    inputs
    {
        item 4 [SupportCorps.CookingPotWithWort;SupportCorps.CookingPotWithMeadWort;SupportCorps.CookingPotWithGrapeMust;SupportCorps.CookingPotWithWhiteGrapeMust;SupportCorps.CookingPotWithPotatoMash;SupportCorps.CookingPotWithGrainMash;SupportCorps.CookingPotWithBerryMust] mappers[FermType],
        item 1 [Base.Yeast;] mode:keep,
        item 1 [Base.Sugar;] mode:destroy,
        item 1 [SupportCorps.WoodenKegWithAirlock;],
    }
    outputs
    {
	item 4 Base.Pot,
        item 1 mapper:FermType,
    }
    itemMapper FermType
    {
        SupportCorps.WoodenKegWithFBeer = SupportCorps.CookingPotWithWort,
        SupportCorps.WoodenKegWithFMead = SupportCorps.CookingPotWithMeadWort,
	SupportCorps.WoodenKegWithFRedWine = SupportCorps.CookingPotWithGrapeMust,
	SupportCorps.WoodenKegWithFWhiteWine = SupportCorps.CookingPotWithWhiteGrapeMust,
	SupportCorps.WoodenKegWithFVodka = SupportCorps.CookingPotWithPotatoMash,
	SupportCorps.WoodenKegWithFBerrywine = SupportCorps.CookingPotWithBerryMust,
    }
}
